## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? -> `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? -> `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? -> `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? -> `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? -> `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search -> read -> references -> definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Incident Debugging: Envoy Connection Pool Exhaustion

## Your Task

A production Envoy proxy is logging `upstream connect error or disconnect/reset before headers. reset reason: overflow`. Trace the error to its source in `envoyproxy/envoy`. Find: 1. The C++ source file that defines the `overflow` reset reason string. 2. The connection pool implementation files under `source/common/conn_pool/` or `source/common/http/` that trigger this overflow condition. 3. The configuration protobuf in `envoyproxy/data-plane-api` that controls `max_connections` and `max_pending_requests` circuit breaker thresholds.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the incident domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)
- `sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6` (envoyproxy/go-control-plane)
- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

2. **The error message** `"upstream connect error or disconnect/reset before headers. reset reason: overflow"` is generated in `source/common/router/router.cc` in the `Filter::onUpstreamReset()` function (lines 1415-1420).

3. **The connection pool overflow trigger** is in `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc`:
   - `ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl()` (line 282-288): checks `pendingRequests().canCreate()` and fires `PoolFailureReason::Overflow` when max pending requests is exceeded
   - `ConnPoolImplBase::attachStreamToClient()` (line 175-181): checks `requests().canCreate()` and fires `PoolFailureReason::Overflow` when max requests is exceeded
   - `ConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnection()` (line 135-138): checks `host_->canCreateConnection(priority_)` which calls `connections().canCreate()` and increments `upstream_cx_overflow_` counter

4. **The HTTP-specific conn pool** is in `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.cc` which extends the base.

5. **The upstream request handler** is in `source/common/router/upstream_request.cc` in `UpstreamRequest::onPoolFailure()` (lines 563-586) which maps `PoolFailureReason::Overflow` to `Http::StreamResetReason::Overflow`.

6. **The configuration protobuf** is in `envoy/config/cluster/v3/circuit_breaker.proto` in the `data-plane-api` repo, specifically the `CircuitBreakers.Thresholds` message with:

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of the findings:

## Key Findings

### 1. The `overflow` reset reason string
- **File**: `source/common/http/utility.cc` — `Utility::resetReasonToString()` returns `"overflow"` for `Http::StreamResetReason::Overflow` (line 1030-1031)
- **Enum definition**: `envoy/http/stream_reset_handler.h` — `StreamResetReason::Overflow` ("The stream was reset because of a resource overflow")
- **Error message assembly**: `source/common/router/router.cc` — `Filter::onUpstreamReset()` builds the full `"upstream connect error or disconnect/reset before headers. reset reason: overflow"` string

### 2. Connection pool overflow implementation
- **`source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc`** — Two overflow trigger points:
  - `newStreamImpl()`: checks `pendingRequests().canCreate()` → fires `PoolFailureReason::Overflow` when `max_pending_requests` exceeded
  - `attachStreamToClient()`: checks `requests().canCreate()` → fires `PoolFailureReason::Overflow` when `max_requests` exceeded
  - `tryCreateNewConnection()`: checks `canCreateConnection()` → increments `upstream_cx_overflow_` when `max_connections` exceeded
- **`source/common/http/conn_pool_base.cc`** — HTTP-specific `HttpConnPoolImplBase` extends the base pool

### 3. Configuration protobuf
- **`envoy/config/cluster/v3/circuit_breaker.proto`** (in `envoyproxy/data-plane-api`) — `CircuitBreakers.Thresholds` message with:
  - `max_connections` (field 2): default 1024
  - `max_pending_requests` (field 3): default 1024
  - `max_requests` (field 4): default 1024
